=== TABLE STRUCTURE: component_marks ===
  id (varchar) NOT NULL
  subject_result_id (varchar) NOT NULL
  enrollment_id (varchar) NOT NULL
  component_id (varchar) NOT NULL
  obtained_marks (numeric) NOT NULL
  total_marks (INTEGER) NOT NULL
  percentage (numeric) NOT NULL
  remarks (TEXT) NULLABLE
  uploaded_by (varchar) NOT NULL
  uploaded_at (datetime) NOT NULL
  created_at (datetime) NULLABLE
  updated_at (datetime) NULLABLE

=== TABLE STRUCTURE: subject_results ===
  id (varchar) NOT NULL
  enrollment_id (varchar) NOT NULL
  subject_id (varchar) NOT NULL
  series_id (varchar) NOT NULL
  grade (varchar) NOT NULL
  pum (numeric) NOT NULL
  total_obtained_marks (numeric) NULLABLE
  total_marks (INTEGER) NULLABLE
  overall_percentage (numeric) NULLABLE
  calculated_uniform_mark (numeric) NULLABLE
  is_passed (tinyint(1)) NOT NULL
  remarks (TEXT) NULLABLE
  status (varchar) NOT NULL
  result_uploaded_at (datetime) NOT NULL
  components_uploaded_at (datetime) NULLABLE
  uploaded_by (varchar) NOT NULL
  created_at (datetime) NULLABLE
  updated_at (datetime) NULLABLE
